# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a Hyperparameter Tuner. You are FORBIDDEN from altering any algorithmic logic, control flow, or adding/removing functions. Your ONLY job is to adjust numeric constants and thresholds.

## Context
We are evolving claude_v6 → claude_v7. The reference bot `bots/bot5/tournament.py` has slightly different anti-lock pressure constants that have been proven through competition. We need to align v7's constants to match bot5's proven values.

## Task: Tune anti-lock pressure constants in `match_pressure_profile` and `apply_anti_lock_pressure`

### In `match_pressure_profile` function:

Find:
```python
    profile["threshold_delta"] = 0.050 * protect - 0.060 * chase
```
Replace with:
```python
    profile["threshold_delta"] = 0.055 * protect - 0.055 * chase
```

### In `apply_anti_lock_pressure` function:

Find these 4 lines:
```python
    match_profile["chase"] = max(match_profile["chase"], 0.85)
    match_profile["threshold_delta"] = min(match_profile["threshold_delta"], -0.070)
    match_profile["sizing_delta"] = max(match_profile["sizing_delta"], 0.16)
    match_profile["bluff_delta"] = max(match_profile["bluff_delta"], 0.11)
```

Replace with:
```python
    match_profile["chase"] = max(match_profile["chase"], 0.90)
    match_profile["threshold_delta"] = min(match_profile["threshold_delta"], -0.075)
    match_profile["sizing_delta"] = max(match_profile["sizing_delta"], 0.18)
    match_profile["bluff_delta"] = max(match_profile["bluff_delta"], 0.13)
```

### Rationale
- **chase 0.85→0.90**: More aggressive chasing when behind in match, better exploitation of opponents playing conservatively.
- **threshold_delta -0.070→-0.075**: Looser call thresholds in anti-lock spots, preventing over-folding when under pressure.
- **sizing_delta 0.16→0.18**: Slightly larger bets when chasing, maximizing fold equity.
- **bluff_delta 0.11→0.13**: More frequent bluffs in anti-lock mode, creating more pressure.
- **threshold_delta formula 0.050/0.060→0.055/0.055**: More symmetric protect/chase balance.

These are the exact values used by bot5 (the highest-rated reference bot).

## IMPORTANT RULES
- DO NOT change any function signatures, add/remove functions, or alter control flow.
- DO NOT modify any files other than `tournament.py`.
- ONLY change the 5 numeric constants listed above.
- Also add `TOTAL_HANDS` to the constants import line (it's imported in bot5 but missing in v6): `from constants import N_PLAYERS, BIG_BLIND, LOCK_WIN_MARGIN, TOTAL_HANDS`
- After editing, verify: `cd bots/claude_v7 && python -c 'import tournament'`

   - Smoke test: `python evolution_workspace/smoke_tester.py bots/claude_v7/main.py`
   - If any check fails, fix the errors before finishing.

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a Hyperparameter Tuner for a Texas Hold'em poker AI bot. Your goal is to OPTIMIZE all numerical thresholds, constants, and magic numbers.

## CRITICAL RULE: DO NOT change algorithmic flow or add new functions.
You may ONLY:
- Change numerical values of constants, thresholds, and weights
- Add new constant definitions (for clarity)
- Adjust multipliers and factors

You may NOT:
- Add new functions or classes
- Change control flow (if/else logic, loops)
- Modify function signatures
- Add new imports

## Setup
1. Wait for Workers 1 and 2 to finish (they're adding algorithmic improvements).
2. Read the FINAL `bots/claude_v7/main.py` that includes all their changes.
3. Also read `bots/bot5/main.py` and `evolution_workspace/experience_pool.md` for context.

## Your Mission: Tune These Categories

### Category 1: Preflop Hand Strength Thresholds
Find and tune all preflop-related constants:
- Opening raise range by position (SB vs BB in heads-up)
- 3-betting threshold (what hands warrant a 3-bet vs just calling)
- Calling a raise threshold
- Fold to 3-bet threshold
- Suggested values to test:
  - Opening raise: top 70-80% of hands from BTN/SB in heads-up
  - 3-bet: top 15-25% of hands
  - Fold to 3-bet: bottom 40-50% of opening range

### Category 2: Bet Sizing Multipliers
Find and tune all bet sizing constants:
- Flop continuation bet size: typically 33-50% pot
- Turn barrel size: typically 50-75% pot
- River value bet size: varies by hand tier (50-150% pot)
- Raise size multipliers: 2.5-3x for value, 2.5-3.5x for bluffs
- Overbet threshold: when to bet >100% pot (strong hands on dry boards)
- Key insight: Smaller c-bets on wet boards, larger on dry boards

### Category 3: Hand Strength Classification Thresholds
Find and tune where hand strength values transition between categories:
- 'monster' threshold: typically 0.85+ (two pair+, sets, straights, flushes)
- 'strong' threshold: typically 0.65-0.85 (top pair good kicker, overpair)
- 'medium' threshold: typically 0.45-0.65 (middle pair, top pair weak kicker)
- 'weak' threshold: typically 0.25-0.45 (bottom pair, gutshots)
- 'trash' threshold: below 0.25

### Category 4: Bluff Frequency Parameters
Find and tune bluff-related constants:
- Base bluff frequency: 20-35% of the time when conditions are met
- Position adjustment: bluff 1.3x more in position than out of position
- Board texture adjustment: bluff 1.5x more on dry boards vs wet
- Street adjustment: bluff 1.5x more on flop, 1.0x on turn, 0.5x on river
- Size adjustment: bluff frequency should decrease with bet size

### Category 5: Pot Odds and Calling Thresholds
Find and tune calling-related constants:
- Minimum equity to call: should be `to_call / (pot + 2 * to_call)` + safety margin
- Safety margin: 3-8% depending on opponent aggression
- Implied odds multiplier: 1.2-1.8x for draws (higher for hidden draws)
- Reverse implied odds penalty: 0.5-0.8x for dominated hands

### Category 6: Monte Carlo Simulation Parameters
Find and tune simulation constants:
- Number of opponent hand samples: 200-500 (more = more accurate but slower)
- Number of community card samples: 50-200 per opponent hand
- Timeout budget: ensure total calculation stays under 2 seconds
- Weight recent opponent actions more heavily: decay factor 0.85-0.95

### Category 7: Opponent Modeling Weights
Find and tune opponent modeling constants:
- VPIP window size: 10-20 hands for initial classification
- Aggression factor thresholds: passive < 1.0, neutral 1.0-2.0, aggressive > 2.0
- Fold to cbet threshold: tight < 40%, average 40-60%, station > 60%
- Weight of showdown evidence vs statistical evidence: 2:1 to 4:1

### Category 8: Position and Stack Depth Weights
Find and tune:
- Position advantage multiplier: 1.1-1.3x for in-position decisions
- Stack-to-pot ratio (SPR) adjustments:
  - SPR < 3: commit with any pair+ draw
  - SPR 3-6: standard play
  - SPR > 6: more cautious, pot control with medium hands
- Blind defense range: top 50-65% of hands

## Tuning Methodology
1. Identify EVERY constant/threshold in the file
2. For each constant, determine if it's reasonable based on poker theory
3. Adjust values toward optimal ranges listed above
4. Use consistent naming: `PREFLOP_OPEN_RANGE`, `CBET_SIZE_DRY_BOARD`, etc.
5. Group all constants at the top of the file or in a dedicated constants section
6. Add comments explaining what each constant does and its valid range

## File Ownership
You are ONLY modifying `bots/claude_v7/main.py`. Do NOT modify any other files.

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a Hyperparameter Tuner for a Texas Hold'em poker bot. You are modifying `bots/claude_v6/tournament.py` ONLY. Your job is to tune the anti-lock pressure parameters to better match bot5's proven values.

## CONTEXT
When the bot is losing badly, `apply_anti_lock_pressure()` overrides the match profile to play more aggressively. The current v6 values are conservative compared to bot5 (the top reference bot).

## YOUR TASK

Read `bots/claude_v6/tournament.py` and find the `apply_anti_lock_pressure` function (around line 145). Currently it reads:
```python
def apply_anti_lock_pressure(match_profile):
    match_profile["protect"] = 0.0
    match_profile["chase"] = max(match_profile["chase"], 0.85)
    match_profile["threshold_delta"] = min(match_profile["threshold_delta"], -0.070)
    match_profile["sizing_delta"] = max(match_profile["sizing_delta"], 0.16)
    match_profile["open_delta"] = min(match_profile["open_delta"], -0.045)
    match_profile["bluff_delta"] = max(match_profile["bluff_delta"], 0.11)
    return match_profile
```

Change it to match bot5's proven values:
```python
def apply_anti_lock_pressure(match_profile):
    match_profile["protect"] = 0.0
    match_profile["chase"] = max(match_profile["chase"], 0.90)
    match_profile["threshold_delta"] = min(match_profile["threshold_delta"], -0.075)
    match_profile["sizing_delta"] = max(match_profile["sizing_delta"], 0.18)
    match_profile["open_delta"] = min(match_profile["open_delta"], -0.045)
    match_profile["bluff_delta"] = max(match_profile["bluff_delta"], 0.13)
    return match_profile
```

Changes made:
- `chase`: 0.85 → 0.90 (more aggressive chasing when behind)
- `threshold_delta`: -0.070 → -0.075 (slightly lower thresholds for action)
- `sizing_delta`: 0.16 → 0.18 (slightly larger bet sizes when desperate)
- `bluff_delta`: 0.11 → 0.13 (more bluffing when behind)
- `open_delta`: -0.045 stays the same (already matches bot5)

## IMPORTANT RULES
- ONLY modify `tournament.py` in `bots/claude_v6/`.
- Do NOT modify any other files.
- Do NOT change any algorithmic logic, function signatures, or control flow.
- ONLY change the 4 numeric constants listed above.
- Verify the file parses: `cd bots/claude_v6 && python3 -c 'import tournament'`

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a [Hyperparameter Tuner] for a Texas Hold'em poker AI (heads-up, no-limit). You are evolving bot claude_v6 → claude_v7.

## Your Mission
Create `bots/claude_v7/constants.py` — a centralized configuration file with all tunable parameters for the v7 bot. Study the claude_v6 bot's hardcoded thresholds and extract them into named constants with v7-optimized values.

## Parameter Categories to Define

### Preflop Parameters
```python
# Opening raise sizes (in BB)
PREFLOP_OPEN_SIZE_SB = 3.0  # SB position opens to 3BB (was likely 2.5)
PREFLOP_OPEN_SIZE_BB = 2.5  # BB position opens to 2.5BB
PREFLOP_3BET_MULTIPLIER = 3.5  # 3bet = 3.5x the opponent's raise
PREFLOP_4BET_MULTIPLIER = 2.8  # 4bet = 2.8x the 3bet
PREFLOP_MIN_3BET_SIZE = 3  # minimum 3bet in BB

# Hand strength tiers for preflop play (0-1 scale from equity simulation)
PREFLOP_PREMIUM_THRESHOLD = 0.85  # AA, KK, QQ, AKs -> always raise/3bet
PREFLOP_STRONG_THRESHOLD = 0.70  # JJ-TT, AQ, AJs -> raise, sometimes 3bet
PREFLOP_PLAYABLE_THRESHOLD = 0.55  # 99-77, ATs+, KQs -> call or raise
PREFLOP_SPECULATIVE_THRESHOLD = 0.45  # suited connectors, small pairs -> call in position
PREFLOP_FOLD_THRESHOLD = 0.35  # everything else -> fold to raises
```

### Postflop Bet Sizing
```python
# Bet sizing as fraction of pot
CBET_SIZE_DRY = 0.33  # small cbet on dry boards
CBET_SIZE_WET = 0.66  # larger cbet on wet boards
VALUE_BET_STRONG = 0.66  # value bet with strong hands
VALUE_BET_MEDIUM = 0.50  # thinner value bet
VALUE_BET_MONSTER_RIVER = 1.2  # overbet river with monsters
BLUFF_SIZE_RIVER = 0.66  # river bluff sizing
DONK_BET_SIZE = 0.50  # donk bet out of position
```

### Bluff Frequency Controls
```python
BASE_BLUFF_FREQUENCY = 0.25  # bluff 25% of air hands in good spots
SEMI_BLUFF_DRAW_FREQUENCY = 0.55  # semi-bluff with strong draws
RIVER_BLUFF_BLOCKER_BONUS = 0.15  # extra bluff% when holding blockers
FLOAT_FREQUENCY = 0.20  # call flop cbet with air planning to take away turn
CHECK_RAISE_BLUFF_FREQ = 0.12  # check-raise bluff frequency
```

### Fold Thresholds
```python
FOLD_TO_3BET_WEAK = 0.75  # fold weak hands to 3bet 75%
FOLD_TO_CBET_WEAK = 0.80  # fold weak hands to cbet 80%
FOLD_TO_RIVER_BET_WEAK = 0.85  # fold weak hands to river bet 85%
CALL_DOWN_MEDIUM_THRESHOLD = 0.45  # call 2 streets with medium if equity > this
```

### Opponent Modeling Thresholds
```python
OPPONENT_VPIP_TIGHT = 0.50  # below = nit
OPPONENT_VPIP_LOOSE = 0.75  # above = calling_station
OPPONENT_PFR_TIGHT = 0.30  # below = passive
OPPONENT_PFR_LOOSE = 0.50  # above = aggressive
OPPONENT_AF_PASSIVE = 1.0  # below = passive
OPPONENT_MIN_HANDS_FOR_MODEL = 5  # minimum hands before trusting model
```

### Stack Size Thresholds
```python
SHORT_STACK_BB = 20  # below this, use push-fold strategy
MEDIUM_STACK_BB = 40  # medium stack play
DEEP_STACK_BB = 80  # deep stack, more speculative play
ALL_IN_THRESHOLD = 15  # below 15BB, consider open-shoving
```

### Match/Endgame Parameters
```python
CHIP_PRESSURE_FACTOR = 0.15  # how much stack deficit affects aggression
ENDGAME_HANDS_REMAINING = 10  # hands left = endgame mode
ENDGAME_AGGRESSION_BOOST = 0.10  # extra aggression in endgame
```

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a Hyperparameter Tuner for a Texas Hold'em poker AI. Your task is to tune constants and thresholds in bots/claude_v6/ (look for constants.py, config.py, or threshold values at the top of the main bot file).

CRITICAL RULE: DO NOT change any algorithmic logic, add new functions, or restructure code. ONLY modify numerical constants, thresholds, and magic numbers.

YOUR TUNING TARGETS:
1. **Preflop Raise Sizing**: If there's a preflop raise size multiplier, test adjusting from current value. Typical range: 2.5x-4x BB for heads-up. Consider position-dependent sizing (smaller on button, larger from BB).

2. **Bluff Frequency Thresholds**: If there are bluff probability thresholds (e.g., bluff when random() < threshold), consider: slightly increasing bluff frequency on dry boards (+0.05-0.10), and decreasing on very wet boards (-0.05-0.10). Total bluff frequency should be in the 20-35% range for heads-up.

3. **Aggression Factor**: If the bot has an aggression parameter, tune it. For heads-up play, higher aggression (1.5-2.5x) typically performs better than passive play.

4. **Continuation Bet Frequency**: Adjust c-bet thresholds. On dry boards, c-bet ~70-80% is strong. On wet boards, consider reducing to ~50-60%.

5. **Value Bet Sizing**: If there are pot-fraction sizing parameters, test: strong hands at 60-80% pot, medium at 40-55%, thin value at 25-35%.

6. **Fold Thresholds**: Tune the minimum hand strength required to call various bet sizes. Against pot-sized bets, folding frequency should be ~50-60%. Against half-pot, ~40-50%.

APPROACH: Read the current constant values first. Make SMALL incremental changes (5-15% adjustments). Document what you changed and why. The goal is marginal improvement, not radical restructuring.

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a Hyperparameter Tuner for a Texas Hold'em poker AI bot.

## Your Mission
Tune parameters, thresholds, and magic numbers in the bot. Source: `bots/claude_v6/`, output: `bots/claude_v7/`.

## CRITICAL RULES
- **FORBIDDEN**: Adding new functions, changing algorithmic logic flow, adding new conditional branches
- **ALLOWED**: Changing numeric constants, thresholds, multipliers, weights, and percentages
- **ALLOWED**: Adding comments explaining why a value was chosen

## Step 1: Read Current Code
Read ALL files in `bots/claude_v6/`. Identify every numeric constant and threshold. Also read `bots/bot5/main.py` for reference parameter values.

## Step 2: Tune Preflop Parameters
In preflop decision logic, adjust:

### 2a. Hand Strength Thresholds
- **Opening range** (first to act): Tune the threshold for which hands to open with. Typical adjustments:
  - UTG (small blind heads-up): Top 70-80% of hands
  - Button (big blind heads-up): Top 80-90% of hands
- **3-bet threshold**: Hands strong enough to re-raise. Typical: Top 15-25%
- **Call 2-bet threshold**: Top 40-60%
- **Fold to 3-bet threshold**: Below top 30-40%

### 2b. Raise Sizing
- **Open raise size**: 2.5-3.5x BB (try 3.0x as baseline, adjust based on position)
- **3-bet size**: 2.5-3.5x the original raise
- **4-bet size**: 2.2-2.8x the 3-bet

## Step 3: Tune Postflop Parameters

### 3a. Bet Sizing
- **Value bet sizing**: On a scale of 0.5-1.0 of pot:
  - Strong hands (two pair+): 0.65-0.85 pot
  - Medium hands (top pair good kicker): 0.5-0.65 pot
  - Weak value (top pair weak kicker): 0.4-0.55 pot
- **Bluff sizing**: 0.5-0.75 pot (must be believable)
- **CBet sizing**: 0.4-0.65 pot on dry boards, 0.55-0.75 on wet boards

### 3b. Fold Equity Thresholds
- **Fold to raise on flop**: Based on hand strength vs board texture. If hand_strength < 0.3 AND board is wet → fold to significant raise
- **Fold to raise on turn**: Tighten to 0.35 threshold
- **Fold to raise on river**: Only continue with made hands > 0.5 strength

### 3c. Pot Odds Thresholds
- Minimum equity to call = (amount_to_call) / (pot_after_calling)
- Add a small margin (1.05-1.15x) to account for implied odds on draws

## Step 4: Tune Endgame Parameters
- **All-in threshold**: Hands strong enough to shove (typically top 10-15% for >30bb, wider for <15bb)
- **Blind defense threshold**: How wide to defend from BB (typically top 55-65%)
- **Steal attempt frequency**: How often to attempt stealing from SB (75-85%)

## Step 5: Document Changes
For each parameter changed, add a comment:
```python
# TUNED: was X, changed to Y because [reason]
```

## Output
Produce the modified files for `bots/claude_v7/`. Ensure all changes are purely numeric threshold/constant adjustments.

You are an Algorithmic Logic Architect for a Texas Hold'em poker AI. Your task is to implement MATCH-PHASE AWARENESS and ENDGAME STRATEGY improvements in the current bot (bots/claude_v6/main.py).

1. evolution_workspace/results/glicko_ratings.json — current ratings

4. bots/bot5/main.py — the reference bot for comparison

THEN implement these specific improvements:

A) **Match Phase Detection**: Add logic to track the current match phase:
   - Early game (hands 1-15): play more conservatively, establish baseline opponent reads
   - Mid game (hands 16-35): exploit accumulated opponent reads, adjust strategy based on chip position
   - Late game (hands 36-45): play more aggressively if behind, protect lead if ahead
   - Endgame (hands 46-50): maximize expected chip equity with ICM-like considerations
   The hand number can be inferred from the request history length.

B) **Chip Position Strategy**: Adjust strategy based on relative chip stacks:
   - If significantly ahead (>60% of total chips): reduce variance, avoid big pots without strong hands
   - If about even (40-60%): play standard strategy with slight aggression
   - If significantly behind (<40%): increase aggression, look for +EV spots to double up
   These thresholds should be configurable (named constants) for the Tuner.

C) **Improved Endgame Push/Fold Logic**: When effective stack sizes are small (<15 big blinds), implement push/fold equilibrium-based play:
   - Calculate the Nash equilibrium pushing range for the current stack depth
   - Use the SAGE system or similar simplified endgame strategy
   - Consider position (button vs blind) when deciding push/fold ranges

- Do NOT change finely-tuned numeric thresholds — use named constants
- Keep all changes within bots/claude_v6/main.py
- Maintain the existing request/response protocol
- Integrate new logic into the existing decision-making pipeline, don't create parallel paths

### Task C: Add Chen preflop strength lookup table
Add the full PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE at the end of constants.py. This is a 169-entry lookup table mapping (high_rank, low_rank, suited) → normalized preflop strength. Port EXACTLY from bot5's constants.py:

```python
PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE = {}
_chen_base = {
    (14,14):1.00,(13,13):0.95,(12,12):0.90,(11,11):0.86,(10,10):0.82,
    (9,9):0.78,(8,8):0.74,(7,7):0.70,(6,6):0.66,(5,5):0.62,
    (4,4):0.58,(3,3):0.55,(2,2):0.52,
    (14,13):0.68,(14,12):0.65,(14,11):0.62,(14,10):0.59,(14,9):0.54,
    (14,8):0.48,(14,7):0.44,(14,6):0.41,(14,5):0.38,(14,4):0.36,
    (14,3):0.35,(14,2):0.34,
    (13,12):0.58,(13,11):0.55,(13,10):0.52,(13,9):0.47,(13,8):0.42,
    (13,7):0.39,(13,6):0.36,(13,5):0.34,(13,4):0.32,(13,3):0.31,
    (13,2):0.30,
    (12,11):0.51,(12,10):0.48,(12,9):0.43,(12,8):0.38,(12,7):0.36,
    (12,6):0.33,(12,5):0.31,(12,4):0.30,(12,3):0.29,(12,2):0.28,
    (11,10):0.45,(11,9):0.40,(11,8):0.36,(11,7):0.34,(11,6):0.31,
    (11,5):0.29,(11,4):0.28,(11,3):0.27,(11,2):0.26,
    (10,9):0.38,(10,8):0.34,(10,7):0.32,(10,6):0.29,(10,5):0.27,
    (10,4):0.26,(10,3):0.25,(10,2):0.24,
    (9,8):0.32,(9,7):0.30,(9,6):0.27,(9,5):0.25,(9,4):0.24,
    (9,3):0.23,(9,2):0.22,
    (8,7):0.29,(8,6):0.26,(8,5):0.24,(8,4):0.23,(8,3):0.22,(8,2):0.21,
    (7,6):0.25,(7,5):0.23,(7,4):0.22,(7,3):0.21,(7,2):0.20,
    (6,5):0.22,(6,4):0.21,(6,3):0.20,(6,2):0.19,
    (5,4):0.21,(5,3):0.20,(5,2):0.19,
    (4,3):0.19,(4,2):0.18,
    (3,2):0.17,
}
for (_h, _l), _v in _chen_base.items():
    if _h == _l:
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = _v
    else:
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.04)
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = max(0.0, _v - 0.02)
        if _h - _l == 1:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.06)
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = _v
        if _h - _l == 2:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.05)
        if _h == 14 and _l >= 10:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.06)
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.02)
```

Replace the ENTIRE estimate_preflop_strength function body with bot5's lookup version:
```python
def estimate_preflop_strength(my_cards):
    r1 = card_number(my_cards[0])
    r2 = card_number(my_cards[1])
    high = max(r1, r2)
    low = min(r1, r2)
    suited = card_suit(my_cards[0]) == card_suit(my_cards[1])
    return PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE.get((high, low, suited), 0.30)
```

This replaces the 20-line formula with a simple lookup. The Chen table provides more accurate preflop hand rankings.

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You

## Context
v6 (r=1420) is 150 points behind bot5 (rank 1). Two critical gaps: (1) v6 uses a simplistic formula for preflop hand evaluation while bot5 uses a precise Chen formula 169-hand lookup table, and (2) v6 has much lower simulation counts. The experience pool confirms these are among the 8 systemic gaps causing the rating deficit.

### 3. ADD Chen formula preflop lookup table:
Copy the ENTIRE PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE dictionary from `bots/bot5/constants.py` and append it to `bots/claude_v6/constants.py`. This is a data-only change — a large dictionary mapping (high_rank, low_rank, suited) to a normalized strength value [0,1] for all 169 distinct preflop hands. The table starts with `PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE = {}` andincludes the `_chen_base` helper dict and the loop that populates the table.

The exact code to append (copy verbatim from bot5/constants.py lines starting at `# Preflop 169-hand Chen formula lookup table`):
```python

# Preflop 169-hand Chen formula lookup table
# Key: (high_rank, low_rank, suited) -> normalized strength [0,1]
PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE = {}
_chen_base = {
    (14,14):1.00,(13,13):0.95,(12,12):0.90,(11,11):0.86,(10,10):0.82,
    (9,9):0.78,(8,8):0.74,(7,7):0.70,(6,6):0.66,(5,5):0.62,
    (4,4):0.58,(3,3):0.55,(2,2):0.52,
    (14,13):0.68,(14,12):0.65,(14,11):0.62,(14,10):0.59,(14,9):0.54,
    (14,8):0.48,(14,7):0.44,(14,6):0.41,(14,5):0.38,(14,4):0.36,
    (14,3):0.35,(14,2):0.34,
    (13,12):0.58,(13,11):0.55,(13,10):0.52,(13,9):0.47,(13,8):0.42,
    (13,7):0.39,(13,6):0.36,(13,5):0.34,(13,4):0.32,(13,3):0.31,
    (13,2):0.30,
    (12,11):0.51,(12,10):0.48,(12,9):0.43,(12,8):0.38,(12,7):0.36,
    (12,6):0.33,(12,5):0.31,(12,4):0.30,(12,3):0.29,(12,2):0.28,
    (11,10):0.45,(11,9):0.40,(11,8):0.36,(11,7):0.34,(11,6):0.31,
    (11,5):0.29,(11,4):0.28,(11,3):0.27,(11,2):0.26,
    (10,9):0.38,(10,8):0.34,(10,7):0.32,(10,6):0.29,(10,5):0.27,
    (10,4):0.26,(10,3):0.25,(10,2):0.24,
    (9,8):0.32,(9,7):0.30,(9,6):0.27,(9,5):0.25,(9,4):0.24,
    (9,3):0.23,(9,2):0.22,
    (8,7):0.29,(8,6):0.26,(8,5):0.24,(8,4):0.23,(8,3):0.22,(8,2):0.21,
    (7,6):0.25,(7,5):0.23,(7,4):0.22,(7,3):0.21,(7,2):0.20,
    (6,5):0.22,(6,4):0.21,(6,3):0.20,(6,2):0.19,
    (5,4):0.21,(5,3):0.20,(5,2):0.19,
    (4,3):0.19,(4,2):0.18,
    (3,2):0.17,
}
for (_h, _l), _v in _chen_base.items():
    if _h == _l:
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = _v
    else:
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.04)
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = max(0.0, _v - 0.02)
        if _h - _l == 1:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.06)
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = _v
        if _h - _l == 2:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.05)
        if _h == 14 and _l >= 10:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.06)
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.02)
```

## CHANGES TO state.py

### 4. UPDATE estimate_preflop_strength() to use Chen table:
Current v6 function:
```python
def estimate_preflop_strength(my_cards):
    r1 = card_number(my_cards[0])
    r2 = card_number(my_cards[1])
    s1 = card_suit(my_cards[0])
    s2 = card_suit(my_cards[1])
    high = max(r1, r2)
    low = min(r1, r2)
    gap = high - low
    suited = s1 == s2
    pair = r1 == r2
    score = 0.0
    score += (high - 2) / 16.0
    score += (low - 2) / 28.0
    if pair:
        score += 0.25 + (high - 2) / 30.0
    else:
        if suited:
            score += 0.06
        if gap == 1:
            score += 0.06
        elif gap == 2:
            score += 0.03
        elif gap >= 4:
            score -= 0.04
    if high == 14:
        score += 0.04
        if low >= 10:
            score += 0.04
    return clamp(score, 0.0, 1.0)
```

Replace the ENTIRE function body with the Chen table lookup (matching bot5):
```python
def estimate_preflop_strength(my_cards):
    r1 = card_number(my_cards[0])
    r2 = card_number(my_cards[1])
    high = max(r1, r2)
    low = min(r1, r2)
    suited = card_suit(my_cards[0]) == card_suit(my_cards[1])
    return PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE.get((high, low, suited), 0.30)
```

### 5. UPDATE state.py imports:
Add `PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE` to the import from constants:
```python
from constants import (
    N_PLAYERS, INITIAL_CHIPS, SMALL_BLIND, BIG_BLIND, TOTAL_HANDS,
    PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE,
)
```

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are an Algorithmic Logic Architect specializing in POSTFLOP DECISION LOGIC for a Texas Hold'em poker AI.

## CRITICAL RULES
- You are FORBIDDEN from changing well-established numeric thresholds. Mark them with `# TUNE:` if you think they need adjustment.
- You may restructure postflop decision logic, add new evaluation branches, and improve existing hand evaluation.
- Do NOT modify files outside bots/claude_v6/main.py.
- Coordinate with Worker 1 (who handles the overall algorithmic architecture). Your focus is specifically on postflop play.

## STEP 1: READ THESE FILES FIRST
1. `bots/claude_v6/main.py` — Current bot code
2. `bots/bot5/main.py` — Best reference bot, STUDY its postflop logic carefully
3. `evolution_workspace/experience_pool.md` — Strategic lessons

## STEP 2: FOCUS AREAS

### A. Multi-Street Hand Strength Progression
Add logic that tracks how hand strength changes from flop → turn → river:
- A strong hand on the flop can become weak if scary cards arrive
- A drawing hand can become strong if it hits
- Implement a `hand_strength_progression()` tracker that adjusts confidence per street

### B. Pot Odds and Expected Value Calculation
Ensure the bot has proper pot odds calculation:
- `calculate_pot_odds(bet_to_call, pot_size)` → returns required equity
- `estimate_equity(hand, board, opponent_range)` → returns estimated win probability
- Decision: call if estimated_equity > pot_odds
- This should be the FOUNDATION of all call/fold decisions postflop

### C. River Play Optimization
River is where the most chips are won/lost. Add specialized river logic:
- **Value betting**: Bet with hands that beat >50% of opponent's calling range
- **Bluff catching**: Call with hands that beat only opponent's bluffs
- **Bluffing**: Only bluff with hands that have zero showdown value AND have good blockers
- **Check-call vs check-fold**: Based on pot odds and opponent's bluffing frequency

### D. Turn Barreling Logic
Second barrel decisions:
- Continue barreling when the turn card improves our range or hurts opponent's range
- Give up bluffs when the turn card is very favorable for opponent
- Double-barrel frequency should be ~40-50% after flop continuation bet

## STEP 3: IMPLEMENT
- Add these as new functions and integrate into the postflop decision flow
- Ensure proper function signatures and clear variable names
- All constants should be marked with `# TUNE:` for the tuner to optimize
- Do NOT break the existing JSON protocol: `{"response": <int>, "data": ...}`

## IMPORTANT: AVOID CONFLICTS WITH WORKER 1
Worker 1 is adding: board texture analysis, draw evaluation, blocker analysis, opponent modeling, and match pressure.
YOU should focus on: multi-street progression, pot odds/EV calculation, river optimization, and turn barreling.
Keep your additions in clearly separate functions to minimize merge conflicts.

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a Hyperparameter Tuner working on a Texas Hold'em poker AI (evolution v6 → v7). Your target files are constants.py and config.py in bots/claude_v6/. 

CRITICAL RULES:
- You MUST NOT add new functions, change algorithmic flow, or restructure logic.
- You MAY ONLY modify numerical constants, thresholds, weight factors, and magic numbers.

Your goal is to tune the following parameters to improve win rate:

1. **Preflop raise sizing**: If the current 3-bet sizing is >3x, reduce to 2.5-3x. Modern optimal preflop sizing trends toward smaller 3-bets. Tune any preflop raise multiplier constants.

2. **C-bet frequency**: Adjust the continuation bet frequency threshold. If currently >70%, reduce to 55-65%. If <50%, increase to 55-65%. C-betting too much or too little is a common leak.

3. **Bluff frequency multipliers**: Reduce overall bluff frequency by 10-15% (multiply bluff probability constants by 0.85-0.90). Most poker bots bluff too frequently. However, ensure river bluff frequency remains slightly higher than flop/turn (river is the most profitable bluff street).

4. **Pot odds calling threshold**: Tighten the pot odds threshold by 3-5%. If the current call threshold is based on equity > pot odds, add a small buffer (require 3-5% more equity than pot odds suggest) to account for implied odds disadvantage.

5. **All-in thresholds**: Increase the minimum hand strength required to go all-in preflop (if there's a threshold for this). A hand that goes all-in preflop should have >55% equity against a reasonable opponent range.

6. **Value bet sizing on strong hands**: If strong hand bet sizing is currently <60% pot, increase to 65-75% pot to extract more value.

Make small, conservative adjustments. After each change, add a comment explaining what was changed and why. Keep a record of old vs new values in comments.

# Action
Please write the Python code to fulfill your objective. After editing:

1. **Verify your changes**: Run `git diff bots/claude_v7/` to review what you changed.
   Ensure no unintended modifications to files outside your assigned `target_files`.
2. If you see unexpected changes, fix them before finishing.

   - If any check fails, fix the errors before finishing.

### 6. Add choose_overbet_river function
Copy this EXACTLY from bots/bot5/strategy.py and add it after choose_preflop_spot_action:

```python
def choose_overbet_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet: 1.5-2.2x pot with NUT hands only."""
    if value_profile is None or value_profile['tier'] != 'nut':
        return None
    if board_texture is not None and board_texture['wetness'] > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None

    pot_after_call = pot + to_call
    ratio = 1.5 + 0.3 * max(0.0, win_rate - 0.70)
    if not spot_info.get('has_position', False):
        ratio = max(1.3, ratio - 0.2)
    ratio = min(ratio, 2.2)
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)

    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2
    amount = min(amount, my_chips - 1)
    if amount <= to_call or amount < min_raise:
        return None
    return amount
```

Also add the disabled bluff version:
```python
def choose_overbet_bluff_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    blocker_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet bluff - disabled for safety."""
    return None
```

```python
    anti_bot4 = get_anti_bot4_adjustments(bot4_score, board_texture, spot_info, round_idx, value_profile)
else:
    anti_bot4 = {
        'bluff_freq_bonus': 0.0, 'raise_size_bonus': 0.0,
        'call_threshold_delta': 0.0, 'fold_threshold_delta': 0.0,
        'river_overbet_enabled': False, 'trap_defense_delta': 0.0,
    }
```

## Task 8: Add river overbet call in get_action

After the anti_bot4 computation, before the repeated_raise_trap logic, add:
```python
if round_idx == 3 and to_call == 0 and len(public_cards) >= 3 and value_profile is not None and value_profile['tier'] == 'nut':
    overbet = choose_overbet_river(
        state['min_raise_action'], my_chips, state['my_round_bet'],
        to_call, pot, win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
    )
    if overbet is not None:
        return overbet
```

## Task 9: Apply anti-bot4 adjustments to thresholds

After computing strong/medium thresholds, add:
```python
strong -= anti_bot4['call_threshold_delta']
medium -= anti_bot4['call_threshold_delta'] * 0.8
strong += anti_bot4['trap_defense_delta']
```

## Task 10: Pass new params to choose_raise calls

In BOTH choose_raise calls in get_action (the one in the to_call > 0 block and the one in the to_call == 0 block), add:
```python
anti_bot4_bonus=anti_bot4['raise_size_bonus'],
allow_river_overbet=anti_bot4.get('river_overbet_enabled', False),
```

## Task 11: Fix allow_low_frequency_blocker_bluff calls

Wherever allow_low_frequency_blocker_bluff is called, add the bluff_freq_bonus param:
```python
allow_low_frequency_blocker_bluff(req, my_cards, public_cards, blocker_profile, round_idx, bluff_freq_bonus=anti_bot4['bluff_freq_bonus'])
```

Copy v6's tournament.py to bots/claude_v7/tournament.py, then make these EXACT changes:

### Change 1: threshold_delta formula (line ~129)
OLD: `profile['threshold_delta'] = 0.050 * protect - 0.060 * chase`
NEW: `profile['threshold_delta'] = 0.055 * protect - 0.055 * chase`

Symmetric coefficients are proven better. The old 0.050/0.060 asymmetry caused chase bias.

### Change 2: anti-lock chase (line ~138)
OLD: `match_profile['chase'] = max(match_profile['chase'], 0.85)`
NEW: `match_profile['chase'] = max(match_profile['chase'], 0.90)`

Higher chase when facing lock loss means more aggressive play when elimination is possible.

### Change 3: anti-lock threshold_delta (line ~139)
OLD: `match_profile['threshold_delta'] = min(match_profile['threshold_delta'], -0.070)`
NEW: `match_profile['threshold_delta'] = min(match_profile['threshold_delta'], -0.075)`

More negative threshold = more willing to continue in anti-lock spots.

### Change 4: anti-lock sizing_delta (line ~140)
OLD: `match_profile['sizing_delta'] = max(match_profile['sizing_delta'], 0.16)`
NEW: `match_profile['sizing_delta'] = max(match_profile['sizing_delta'], 0.18)`

Larger sizing in anti-lock pressure = more aggressive bet sizing.

### Change 5: anti-lock bluff_delta (line ~142)
OLD: `match_profile['bluff_delta'] = max(match_profile['bluff_delta'], 0.11)`
NEW: `match_profile['bluff_delta'] = max(match_profile['bluff_delta'], 0.13)`

Higher bluff delta = more willingness to bluff when facing elimination.

## Task 5: strategy.py — Add choose_overbet_river and choose_overbet_bluff_river

Copy these two functions EXACTLY from bots/bot5/strategy.py (lines 453-485). Place them AFTER choose_raise and BEFORE choose_preflop_spot_action:

```python
def choose_overbet_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet: 1.5-2.2x pot with NUT hands only."""
    if value_profile is None or value_profile["tier"] != "nut":
        return None
    if board_texture is not None and board_texture["wetness"] > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None

    pot_after_call = pot + to_call
    ratio = 1.5 + 0.3 * max(0.0, win_rate - 0.70)
    if not spot_info.get("has_position", False):
        ratio = max(1.3, ratio - 0.2)
    ratio = min(ratio, 2.2)
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)

    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2
    amount = min(amount, my_chips - 1)
    if amount <= to_call or amount < min_raise:
        return None
    return amount


def choose_overbet_bluff_river(
    min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot,
    blocker_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model
):
    """River overbet bluff - disabled for safety."""
    return None
```

```python
            target = int(to_call + pot_after_call * 0.75)
            target = max(target, state["min_raise_action"])
            if target >= my_chips * 0.5:
                return -2
            return target

        if 0.38 <= preflop_strength <= 0.52 and confidence >= 0.25 and fold_to_raise > 0.45:
            hand_index = get_hand_index(req) or 0
            token = (sum(req["my_cards"]) * 13 + hand_index * 7) % 100
            bluff_freq = clamp((fold_to_raise - 0.45) * 1.2, 0, 0.6)
            if token < int(bluff_freq * 100):
                target = int(to_call + pot_after_call * 0.60)
                target = max(target, state["min_raise_action"])
                if target >= my_chips:
                    return -2

        call_threshold = 0.42 + match_adjust - loose_bonus
```


### 8f. Pass anti_bot4 to choose_raise calls
Find ALL calls to `choose_raise(` in get_action and add these two parameters:

```python
allow_river_overbet=anti_bot4["river_overbet_enabled"],
```

```python

```

### 8h. Apply anti_bot4 to bluff/probe/semi_bluff thresholds
Find where `river_bluff_threshold`, `probe_fold_threshold`, `semi_bluff_threshold` are calculated and subtract `anti_bot4["bluff_freq_bonus"]` from each:
```python
river_bluff_threshold = 0.62 - 0.28 * match_profile["bluff_delta"] - anti_bot4["bluff_freq_bonus"]
probe_fold_threshold = 0.56 - 0.32 * match_profile["bluff_delta"] - anti_bot4["bluff_freq_bonus"]
semi_bluff_threshold = 0.58 - 0.28 * match_profile["bluff_delta"] - anti_bot4["bluff_freq_bonus"]
```
Also update the bluff/probe guard conditions that check `anti_bot4["bluff_freq_bonus"] < 0.05`:
```python
and anti_bot4["bluff_freq_bonus"] < 0.05  # allow bluffs when bot_4 detected
```
These guards should allow bluffs through when bot4 is detected (bluff_freq_bonus >= 0.05).

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a Hyperparameter Tuner for a Texas Hold'em poker AI. Your job is to optimize constants, thresholds, and magic numbers. You are FORBIDDEN from altering any algorithmic flow, adding new functions, or changing control logic.

## Context
The bot plays heads-up No-Limit Texas Hold'em. Current evolution: claude_v6 → claude_v7. Parameters that typically affect winrate most:
- Preflop opening ranges (hand strength thresholds per position)
- Postflop aggression levels (bet/raise frequency multipliers)
- Bluff frequencies (how often to bluff on each street)
- Pot odds calling thresholds (minimum equity needed to call)
- Sizing ratios (fraction of pot for value bets vs bluffs)
- Fold-to-raise thresholds (hand strength needed to call a raise)

## Your Mission
1. **Read bots/claude_v6/main.py** — identify ALL tunable constants, thresholds, and magic numbers. These typically appear as:
   - Numeric literals in conditional expressions (e.g., `if equity > 0.65`)
   - Named constants at the top of the file (e.g., `BLUFF_FREQ = 0.3`)
   - Multipliers in calculations (e.g., `bet_size = pot * 0.75`)

2. **Read bots/bot5/main.py** — compare its thresholds with v6's. Note where bot5 uses different values for the same concept.

3. **Copy bots/claude_v6/main.py to bots/claude_v7/main.py** and adjust parameters as follows:

   a. **Preflop thresholds**: Tighten opening range slightly in early position, widen in late position (button). If v6 uses a single threshold for all positions, add position awareness.

   b. **Postflop aggression**: Increase c-bet frequency on dry boards by ~5%. Decrease c-bet frequency on wet boards by ~5%. This exploits the common adjustment pattern of opponents.

   c. **Bluff sizing**: On the river, use polarized sizing — bluffs should bet SMALLER (40-50% pot) when they are pure bluffs, and LARGER (75-90% pot) when value betting. This creates a harder-to-exploit strategy.

   d. **Pot odds thresholds**: Lower the calling threshold by ~2-3 percentage points on the flop (call with slightly worse equity since there are 2 streets to improve). Raise the calling threshold by ~2-3 percentage points on the river (need stronger hand since no more cards to improve).

   e. **Fold-to-3bet thresholds**: If v6 folds too much to 3bets, lower the fold threshold by 5%. Position matters — fold less on the button, more out of position.

4. **CRITICAL RULES**:
   - ONLY modify numeric constants, thresholds, and literal values
   - DO NOT add new functions, classes, or control flow statements
   - DO NOT change the JSON I/O protocol
   - DO NOT modify any import statements
   - Keep ALL existing logic structure identical — only change the numbers
   - Add comments next to each changed constant explaining the rationale (e.g., `# v6: 0.65, lowered to improve flop call EV`)

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a Hyperparameter Tuner evolving a Texas Hold'em poker bot from claude_v6 to claude_v7.

## Setup
1. Read `evolution_workspace/results/glicko_ratings.json` to understand current ratings.
2. Read `evolution_workspace/experience_pool.md` for tuning lessons from past iterations.
3. Read `bots/claude_v6/main.py` and identify ALL constants, thresholds, and magic numbers.
4. Read `bots/bot5/main.py` to compare parameter values used by the strongest reference bot.
5. Run `git diff bot-v5 bot-v6 -- bots/` to see what parameters changed last evolution.

## Your Mission: Tune Constants and Thresholds

**CRITICAL: You are FORBIDDEN from altering algorithmic logic, adding new functions, or changing control flow. ONLY modify constants, thresholds, and magic numbers.**

### Task 1: Extract and Organize Constants
If constants are scattered throughout the code, extract them into a dedicated `constants.py` file (or section). Organize by category:

### Task 2: Tune Preflop Parameters
Compare current values with bot5's values and poker theory. Adjust:
- **Opening range by position**: SB opening range, BB opening range (in heads-up, both are in-position for different streets)
- **3-bet frequency**: Base probability of 3-betting with different hand strengths (premium: AA-TT/AK, strong: 99-77/AQ, speculative: suited connectors)
- **Fold to 3-bet thresholds**: What hand strength threshold to continue vs a 3-bet
- **Preflop raise sizing**: Base multiplier (typically 2.5-3.5x BB for heads-up)
- **Limp/stab frequency**: How often to limp (if strategy includes limping) and stab at pots

### Task 3: Tune Postflop Parameters
- **Bet sizing fractions**: 
  - Value bet sizes: try 50-75% pot (currently might be too large or too small)
  - Bluff bet sizes: try 50-80% pot (needs to be credible)
  - Continuation bet size: try 33-50% pot on dry boards, 50-75% on wet boards
- **Check-raise frequency**: Base probability (typically 8-15% of checks)
- **Fold equity thresholds**: Minimum estimated fold probability to justify a bluff (typically 30-45%)
- **Draw continuation thresholds**: Minimum draw strength (outs count) to continue with a draw
- **Pot odds call threshold**: How tight/loose to call based on pot odds (e.g., need 35%+ equity to call)

### Task 4: Tune Aggression and Bluffing Parameters
- **Bluff frequency caps**: Maximum bluff frequency per street (preflop: 15-25%, flop: 20-35%, turn: 15-25%, river: 10-20%)
- **Semi-bluff threshold**: Minimum number of outs to justify a semi-bluff raise (typically 8+ outs)
- **Barrel frequency**: How often to fire a second barrel on the turn after a flop c-bet (30-50%)
- **Triple barrel frequency**: How often to fire all three streets as a bluff (5-15%)

### Task 5: Tune Endgame Parameters
- **Short stack adjustment threshold**: Chip count below which to switch to push/fold (typically < 15-20 BB)
- **Match pressure aggression multiplier**: When behind in the match, how much to increase aggression (1.2-1.5x)
- **Match lead protection multiplier**: When ahead, how much to reduce variance (0.7-0.9x)

### Tuning Methodology:
1. For each parameter, note the current value, bot5's value (if applicable), and your proposed value
2. Make CONSERVATIVE adjustments — change each parameter by at most 20% from current value
3. If a parameter is already well-tuned (close to theoretical optimum), leave it unchanged
4. Add comments explaining WHY each value was chosen
5. If unsure about a parameter, err on the side of not changing it

### Critical Rules:
- DO NOT write new functions, classes, or algorithmic logic
- DO NOT change if/else conditions, loop structures, or control flow
- ONLY modify numeric values: thresholds, multipliers, frequencies, percentages
- Keep all constants in `constants.py` (or the designated constants section)
- Ensure every changed constant has a comment explaining the rationale

Change to symmetric weights:
```python

```

   Also remove the `and to_call == 0` guard from the thin_control condition if it exists (bot5 does NOT have this guard).
4. Fix max_ratio: Change `ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, 1.45)` to:
   ```python
   max_ratio = 2.2 if (allow_river_overbet and round_idx == 3 and value_profile.get('tier') == 'nut') else 1.45
   ratio = clamp(ratio, low_ratio, max_ratio)
   ```

### C. Add choose_overbet_river() Function
Copy this EXACT function from bots/bot5/strategy.py:
```python
def choose_overbet_river(min_raise, my_chips, my_round_bet, to_call, pot, win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model):
    """River overbet: 1.5-2.2x pot with NUT hands only."""
    if value_profile is None or value_profile['tier'] != 'nut':
        return None
    if board_texture is not None and board_texture['wetness'] > 0.35:
        return None
    if pot < 400:
        return None
    pot_after_call = pot + to_call
    ratio = 1.5 + 0.3 * max(0.0, win_rate - 0.70)
    if not spot_info.get('has_position', False):
        ratio = max(1.3, ratio - 0.2)
    ratio = min(ratio, 2.2)
    amount = int(to_call + pot_after_call * ratio)
    if amount >= my_chips:
        return -2
    amount = min(amount, my_chips - 1)
    if amount <= to_call or amount < min_raise:
        return None
    return amount
```
Integrate it into get_action(): Before the final `return 0` at the end of get_action(), add a river overbet check:
```python
if round_idx == 3 and to_call == 0 and value_profile and value_profile['tier'] == 'nut' and anti_bot4 and anti_bot4.get('river_overbet_enabled'):
    overbet = choose_overbet_river(state['min_raise_action'], my_chips, state['my_round_bet'], to_call, pot, win_rate, value_profile, board_texture, spot_info, opponent_model)
    if overbet is not None:
        return overbet
```

### D. Fix realized_postflop_equity()
1. Remove the `pot` parameter entirely from the function signature.
2. Remove the `big_pot` variable and all `big_pot` references.
3. Fix air hand EQR: Change `0.68 if has_position else 0.56` to `0.72 if has_position else 0.62`.
4. Fix air lower bound: Change `0.40` to `0.45`.
5. In the draw OOP branch (draw_strength >= 0.08 and made_strength < 0.18 and not has_position): Remove the `big_pot` subtraction entirely.
6. In pair EQR: Change `0.84 if has_position else 0.73` to `0.86 if has_position else 0.78`.
7. In the pair branch: Remove the `if not has_position: eqr -= 0.05` extra OOP subtraction on double barrel.
8. Update all callers of realized_postflop_equity to remove the `pot=pot` argument.

## CRITICAL RULES
- Do NOT modify constants.py, card_utils.py, state.py, opponent.py, postflop.py, or tournament.py — other workers handle those.
- Copy choose_overbet_river EXACTLY from bot5.

# Master Architect's Specific Prompt For You
You are a Hyperparameter Tuner for a Texas Hold'em poker AI (claude_v7). Your target file is bots/claude_v6/constants.py (save output as bots/claude_v7/constants.py).

CONTEXT: This bot plays heads-up No-Limit Texas Hold'em on Botzone. The constants file contains all the tuned thresholds, percentages, and multipliers that control the bot's behavior.

YOUR MISSION: Tune and optimize the hyperparameters. You are FORBIDDEN from changing any algorithmic logic, function signatures, or code structure. ONLY modify numeric constants, thresholds, and magic numbers.

Specific tuning targets:

1. **Preflop raise sizing**: If there are constants controlling preflop raise sizes (e.g., 3x BB, 2.5x BB), experiment with slightly smaller raises in position (2.2-2.5x) and slightly larger out of position (3-3.5x). Heads-up NLHE favors smaller opens in position.

2. **Bluff frequency thresholds**: If there are bluff probability thresholds (e.g., bluff when hand strength < 0.3), consider adjusting: (a) decrease bluff frequency slightly on dry boards (0.25), (b) increase bluff frequency on wet/draw-heavy boards (0.35), (c) make river bluffs more selective — only bluff with hands that have zero showdown value.

3. **Fold equity thresholds**: If there are fold equity calculations, tighten the thresholds: (a) require higher fold equity (add 5-10%) before making bluff raises, (b) reduce call-station tendencies by folding slightly more marginal hands (e.g., if the bot calls with top pair weak kicker, make it fold weak kickers more often).

4. **Value betting thresholds**: (a) Slightly widen value betting range on safe boards (bet with medium-strength hands more often when board is dry), (b) Tighten value betting range on dangerous boards (only bet with strong hands when many draws are possible).

5. **Stack-preservation thresholds**: Ensure the bot doesn't commit too large a portion of its stack with marginal hands. If there are stack-commit thresholds, make them slightly more conservative (e.g., if the bot commits with >40% stack, change to >35% requiring stronger hands).

6. **Opponent modeling decay rates**: If there are constants controlling how quickly opponent statistics update, ensure they're balanced — not too reactive to small samples (minimum 10 hands before trusting stats) but responsive enough to catch aggressive/passive patterns.

CRITICAL RULES:
- DO NOT add new functions, classes, or algorithmic logic.
- DO NOT modify any code structure or control flow.
- ONLY change numeric values (integers, floats) in the constants/config.
- Document each change with a comment explaining WHY the new value was chosen.
- Keep the file's overall structure and organization identical.
- If a constant doesn't exist, DO NOT create new ones — only tune what's already there.

```python
# Precomputed card number and suit for all 52 cards
CARD_RANKS = [c // 4 + 2 for c in range(52)]
CARD_SUITS = [c % 4 for c in range(52)]

# Preflop 169-hand Chen formula lookup table
# Key: (high_rank, low_rank, suited) -> normalized strength [0,1]
PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE = {}
_chen_base = {
    (14,14):1.00,(13,13):0.95,(12,12):0.90,(11,11):0.86,(10,10):0.82,

    (13,12):0.58,(13,11):0.55,(13,10):0.52,(13,9):0.47,(13,8):0.42,
    (13,7):0.39,(13,6):0.36,(13,5):0.34,(13,4):0.32,(13,3):0.31,
    (13,2):0.30,
    (12,11):0.51,(12,10):0.48,(12,9):0.43,(12,8):0.38,(12,7):0.36,
    (12,6):0.33,(12,5):0.31,(12,4):0.30,(12,3):0.29,(12,2):0.28,
    (11,10):0.45,(11,9):0.40,(11,8):0.36,(11,7):0.34,(11,6):0.31,
    (11,5):0.29,(11,4):0.28,(11,3):0.27,(11,2):0.26,
    (10,9):0.38,(10,8):0.34,(10,7):0.32,(10,6):0.29,(10,5):0.27,
    (10,4):0.26,(10,3):0.25,(10,2):0.24,
    (9,8):0.32,(9,7):0.30,(9,6):0.27,(9,5):0.25,(9,4):0.24,
    (9,3):0.23,(9,2):0.22,
    (8,7):0.29,(8,6):0.26,(8,5):0.24,(8,4):0.23,(8,3):0.22,(8,2):0.21,
    (7,6):0.25,(7,5):0.23,(7,4):0.22,(7,3):0.21,(7,2):0.20,
    (6,5):0.22,(6,4):0.21,(6,3):0.20,(6,2):0.19,
    (5,4):0.21,(5,3):0.20,(5,2):0.19,
    (4,3):0.19,(4,2):0.18,
    (3,2):0.17,

for (_h, _l), _v in _chen_base.items():
    if _h == _l:
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = _v
    else:
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.04)
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = max(0.0, _v - 0.02)
        if _h - _l == 1:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.06)
```

### 1c: Add PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE (Chen formula lookup)
Add this ENTIRE block at the end of constants.py. Copy it EXACTLY from `bots/bot5/constants.py`:

```python
# Preflop 169-hand Chen formula lookup table
# Key: (high_rank, low_rank, suited) -> normalized strength [0,1]
PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE = {}
_chen_base = {
    (14,14):1.00,(13,13):0.95,(12,12):0.90,(11,11):0.86,(10,10):0.82,
    (9,9):0.78,(8,8):0.74,(7,7):0.70,(6,6):0.66,(5,5):0.62,
    (4,4):0.58,(3,3):0.55,(2,2):0.52,
    (14,13):0.68,(14,12):0.65,(14,11):0.62,(14,10):0.59,(14,9):0.54,
    (14,8):0.48,(14,7):0.44,(14,6):0.41,(14,5):0.38,(14,4):0.36,
    (14,3):0.35,(14,2):0.34,
    (13,12):0.58,(13,11):0.55,(13,10):0.52,(13,9):0.47,(13,8):0.42,
    (13,7):0.39,(13,6):0.36,(13,5):0.34,(13,4):0.32,(13,3):0.31,
    (13,2):0.30,
    (12,11):0.51,(12,10):0.48,(12,9):0.43,(12,8):0.38,(12,7):0.36,
    (12,6):0.33,(12,5):0.31,(12,4):0.30,(12,3):0.29,(12,2):0.28,
    (11,10):0.45,(11,9):0.40,(11,8):0.36,(11,7):0.34,(11,6):0.31,
    (11,5):0.29,(11,4):0.28,(11,3):0.27,(11,2):0.26,
    (10,9):0.38,(10,8):0.34,(10,7):0.32,(10,6):0.29,(10,5):0.27,
    (10,4):0.26,(10,3):0.25,(10,2):0.24,
    (9,8):0.32,(9,7):0.30,(9,6):0.27,(9,5):0.25,(9,4):0.24,
    (9,3):0.23,(9,2):0.22,
    (8,7):0.29,(8,6):0.26,(8,5):0.24,(8,4):0.23,(8,3):0.22,(8,2):0.21,
    (7,6):0.25,(7,5):0.23,(7,4):0.22,(7,3):0.21,(7,2):0.20,
    (6,5):0.22,(6,4):0.21,(6,3):0.20,(6,2):0.19,
    (5,4):0.21,(5,3):0.20,(5,2):0.19,
    (4,3):0.19,(4,2):0.18,
    (3,2):0.17,
}
for (_h, _l), _v in _chen_base.items():
    if _h == _l:
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = _v
    else:
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.04)
        PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = max(0.0, _v - 0.02)
        if _h - _l == 1:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.06)
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = _v
        if _h - _l == 2:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.05)
        if _h == 14 and _l >= 10:
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, True)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.06)
            PREFLOP_STRENGTH_TABLE[(_h, _l, False)] = min(1.0, _v + 0.02)
```

Current v6 values → bot5 values:
```python
def apply_anti_lock_pressure(match_profile):
    match_profile["protect"] = 0.0
    match_profile["chase"] = max(match_profile["chase"], 0.90)      # was 0.85
    match_profile["threshold_delta"] = min(match_profile["threshold_delta"], -0.075)  # was -0.070
    match_profile["sizing_delta"] = max(match_profile["sizing_delta"], 0.18)   # was 0.16
    match_profile["open_delta"] = min(match_profile["open_delta"], -0.045)
    match_profile["bluff_delta"] = max(match_profile["bluff_delta"], 0.13)     # was 0.11
    return match_profile
```

### Change 4: Fix threshold_delta in match_pressure_profile

Current: `profile["threshold_delta"] = 0.050 * protect - 0.060 * chase`
Fix to: `profile["threshold_delta"] = 0.055 * protect - 0.055 * chase`

This makes the threshold delta symmetric between protect and chase.
